## Base models
### 1. Do youth with familial risk for SMI display higher brain age?

#### 1.1 Effect of familial risk

<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuZ3JvdXBfbW9kIDwtIGxtZXIoY29ycmVjdGVkX2JyYWluX2FnZV9nYXAgfiBncm91cCArIHBvbHkoY2hyb25vbG9naWNhbF9hZ2UsIDIpICsgc2V4XG4gICsgKDEgfCBzY2FuX2lkKSArICgxIHwgZmlkKSwgZGF0YSA9IGZyYikgI3BvbHkgPSBwb2x5bm9taWFscyAoaS5lLiwgYWdlLCBhZ2Ugc3F1YXJlZClcbiMgcG9seW5vbWlhbCBhZ2UgdmFyaWFibGUgY2FwdHVyZXMgdGhlIG5vbi1saW5lYXIgcmVsYXRpb25zaGlwIGJldHdlZW4gYWdlIGFuZCBicmFpbmFnZSBnYXBcblxuanRvb2xzOjpzdW1tKGdyb3VwX21vZCwgc2NhbGUgPSBGQUxTRSwgdHJhbnNmb3JtLnJlc3BvbnNlID0gVCwgY29uZmludCA9IFQpXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r
group_mod <- lmer(corrected_brain_age_gap ~ group + poly(chronological_age, 2) + sex
  + (1 | scan_id) + (1 | fid), data = frb) #poly = polynomials (i.e., age, age squared)
# polynomial age variable captures the non-linear relationship between age and brainage gap

#### 1.2 Effect of MDD diagnosis


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxubWRkX21vZCA8LSBsbWVyKGNvcnJlY3RlZF9icmFpbl9hZ2VfZ2FwIH4gY2xtZGQgKyBwb2x5KGNocm9ub2xvZ2ljYWxfYWdlLCAyKSArIHNleFxuICArICgxIHwgc2Nhbl9pZCkgKyAoMSB8IGZpZCksIGRhdGEgPSBmcmIpICNwb2x5ID0gcG9seW5vbWlhbHMgKGkuZS4sIGFnZSwgYWdlIHNxdWFyZWQpXG4jIHBvbHlub21pYWwgYWdlIHZhcmlhYmxlIGNhcHR1cmVzIHRoZSBub24tbGluZWFyIHJlbGF0aW9uc2hpcCBiZXR3ZWVuIGFnZSBhbmQgYnJhaW5hZ2UgZ2FwXG5cbmp0b29sczo6c3VtbShtZGRfbW9kLCBzY2FsZSA9IEZBTFNFLCB0cmFuc2Zvcm0ucmVzcG9uc2UgPSBULCBjb25maW50ID0gVClcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
mdd_mod <- lmer(corrected_brain_age_gap ~ clmdd + poly(chronological_age, 2) + sex

```r

all_mod <- lmer(adjusted_brain_age_gap ~ poly(chronological_age, 2) + 
                sex + group + clmdd + clbpd + psy_ant + anx_ant + cladhd + iq + (1 | scan_id) + (1 | fid), 
                data = frb)

```

  • none of the variables are significant after being in the same model due to likely high correlation

3. Do youth with familial risk for SMI who also have the above antecedents display a positive brain age gap, and does it significantly differ from youth without familial risk or antecedent traits?
